e5b31053-df3f-11e6-8f37-fa163e345ce9,mixedbit.speechtrainer,great concept but some problems I have used this app for 5+ hrs and think its a great tool. However  there are a few limitations. If you use this where you have any sort of background noise  it does not work properly. If you speak long sentences really slowly  it plays back the recording before the spoken sentence is complete. Also  the app does not run in the background. If you are able to find a quiet place and your goal is speech training for words or short phrases  this is a good choice. However  in sub optimal environments  and depending on how you plan to do speech training  it might not be the right one. I prefer EchoHacks Speech Trainer for longer sentence drills. It is more resistant to background noise  and gives me control how many seconds I want to echo. I am using both Speech Trainers for different purposes as they have different strength and weaknesses.,June 07 2012,4,1949
